##Second Age Begins in 593, Third Age begins in 4033##

#### Tumakveh Dynasty ####
## The Kings of Bellakar
## The Pretender-Kings of Bellazen

### Lords of Bellakar ###
# Lords of Korlea
# Line of Ishtraraza, Lords of Bur Esmer, stewards of the Ishra Cult
# Lords of Urezayan
# Lords of Har Shulam
# Lords of Siresani

	trait = temperate
	trait = saint
    trait = theologian
    trait = scholar
    trait = diplomat
	
	4805.8.2 = {
		birth = yes
        effect = {	
            add_trait = blood_of_numenor_6
        }
	}
    4900.1.1 = {
        give_nickname = nick_the_prophet_saint
        effect = {
            add_character_flag = {
                flag = had_nickname_event
            }
            save_scope_as = saint_prophet
        }
    }	
	4927.8.12 = { 
		death = {
			death_reason = death_battle
		}	
	}
}
